)\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}}\label{namespaceBotan_aaafcd26fc5a710d6c4656e1201d4d1be}
Verify primality -\/ this function is slow but useful if you want to ensure that a possibly malicious entity did not provide you with something that 'looks like' a prime 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em n} & a positive integer to test for primality \\
\hline
{\em rng} & a random number generator \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
true if all primality tests passed, otherwise false 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{namespaceBotan_a016ece4183f967295bdc54627bb40821}{\index{Botan@{Botan}!version\-\_\-datestamp@{version\-\_\-datestamp}}
\index{version\-\_\-datestamp@{version\-\_\-datestamp}!Botan@{Botan}}
\subsubsection[{version\-\_\-datestamp}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}B\-O\-T\-A\-N\-\_\-\-D\-L\-L {\bf u32bit} Botan\-::version\-\_\-datestamp (
\begin{DoxyParamCaption}
{}
\end{DoxyParamCaption}
)}}\label{namespaceBotan_a016ece4183f967295bdc54627bb40821}
Return the date this version of botan was released, in an integer of the form Y\-Y\-Y\-Y\-M\-M\-D\-D. For instance a version released on May 21, 2013 would return the integer 20130521. If the currently running version is not an official release, this function will return 0 instead.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
release date, or zero if unreleased 
\end{DoxyReturn}
